	var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");

	}
}

<div id="countdown-placeholderCE">
<!-- countdown -->
<style>
	.countdown-cont{width:110%;margin:15px -5% 0;text-align:center;}
	.countdown{padding:5px 5%;border:solid #ce3f51 1px;border-radius:8px;display:inline-block;}
	.countdown > div{display:inline-block;box-sizing:border-box;}
	.countdown .number{padding:2px;margin-left:0;font-size:28px;font-weight:700;display:inline-block;text-align:center;color:#ce3f51;}
	.countdown .label{padding:2px 0 2px 0;font-size:12px;font-weight:400;text-align:center;display:block;color:#666;}
	.countdown .sep{display:inline-block;vertical-align:top;font-size:30px;font-weight:700;color:#666;}
	.countdown .sep::after{content:":";font-weight:normal;}
	@media screen and (max-width:1023px) {
		.countdown{padding:5px 3%;}
		.countdown .number, .countdown .sep{font-size:18px;}
	}
</style>
<div class="countdown-cont">
<div class="countdown CE">
<div class="days">
<span class="number">1</span>
<span class="number">4</span>
<span class="label">DAYS</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="hours">
<span class="number">1</span>
<span class="number">7</span>
<span class="label">HOURS</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="mins">
<span class="number">2</span>
<span class="number">5</span>
<span class="label">MINUTES</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="secs">
<span class="number">2</span>
<span class="number">9</span>
<span class="label">SECONDS</span>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<script>
(function(){
	var 
		FOCUS_EVENT_DELAY = 10000,
		RESYNC_INTERVAL = 10*60000;
	
	var 
		show = "CE",
		days = 14,
		hours = 17,
		mins = 25,
		secs = 30,
		intervalId = null,
		resyncIntervalId = null;
		
	function formatNumber(elem, n) {
		elem[0].innerHTML = Math.floor(n / 10);
		elem[1].innerHTML = n % 10;
	}
		
	function countdown() {
		
		if(days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins == 0) {
			clearInterval(intervalId); return;
		}
		
		--secs;
		if(secs < 0) {
			secs = 59;
			--mins;
		}
		if(mins < 0) { mins = 59; --hours; }
		if(hours < 0){ hours = 23;--days; }
		if(days < 0) { days = 0; }
		
		updateCountdownHTML();
		
		if(days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins <= 5) {
			clearInterval(intervalId);
			/* Remove countdown once time reaches 4 mins */
			$("#countdown-placeholder"+show).html("");
			$(".TS_CE .GS_TS_btn").css("bottom", "100px");
			return;
		}
	}
	
	function updateCountdownHTML() {
		var 
			daysElem = document.querySelectorAll(".CE .days .number"),
			hoursElem = document.querySelectorAll(".CE .hours .number"),
			minsElem = document.querySelectorAll(".CE .mins .number"),
			secsElem = document.querySelectorAll(".CE .secs .number");

		try{
			formatNumber(daysElem, days);
			formatNumber(hoursElem, hours);
			formatNumber(minsElem, mins);
			formatNumber(secsElem, secs);
		}
		catch(ex) {
			/* In case there are still tasks on the event queue when 
			we replace the script during a resync */
		}
		
	}
	
	var dontCount = (days < 0 || hours < 0 || mins < 0) || (days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins == 0);
	if(dontCount) {
		days = 0; hours = 0; mins = 0;
		updateCountdownHTML();
		return;
	}
		
	intervalId = setInterval(countdown, 1000);
	
	function fetchCountdown() {		
		$.ajax({  
				type: "GET",
				url : "/gsol/SITE/JSP/HOMEPAGE-TS-COUNTDOWN.jsp?show="+show,
				dataType : "html",
				async: true,
				success: function(data){
					/* About to replace the script - clear all existing tasks in event queue */
					clearInterval(intervalId);
					clearInterval(resyncIntervalId);
					$("#countdown-placeholder"+show).html(data);
				}
			});
	}
	
	/* Re-synchronize on window focus */
	$(window).on("focus", function(){
		if(window["ST_focusIntervalId_CE"]) { 
			return; 
		}
		else {
			fetchCountdown();
			window["ST_focusIntervalId_CE"] = 
				setTimeout(function(){ window["ST_focusIntervalId_CE"] = null; }, FOCUS_EVENT_DELAY);
		}
	});
	
	/* Re-synchronize every 10 minutes */
	resyncIntervalId = setInterval(fetchCountdown, RESYNC_INTERVAL);
	
})();
</script>
</div>

</div>
</div>

<script>
(function(){
	var 
		FOCUS_EVENT_DELAY = 10000,
		RESYNC_INTERVAL = 10*60000;
	
	var 
		show = "ME",
		days = 21,
		hours = 17,
		mins = 55,
		secs = 30,
		intervalId = null,
		resyncIntervalId = null;
		
	function formatNumber(elem, n) {
		elem[0].innerHTML = Math.floor(n / 10);
		elem[1].innerHTML = n % 10;
	}
		
	function countdown() {
		
		if(days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins == 0) {
			clearInterval(intervalId); return;
		}
		
		--secs;
		if(secs < 0) {
			secs = 59;
			--mins;
		}
		if(mins < 0) { mins = 59; --hours; }
		if(hours < 0){ hours = 23;--days; }
		if(days < 0) { days = 0; }
		
		updateCountdownHTML();
		
		if(days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins <= 5) {
			clearInterval(intervalId);
			/* Remove countdown once time reaches 4 mins */
			$("#countdown-placeholder"+show).html("");
			$(".TS_ME .GS_TS_btn").css("bottom", "100px");
			return;
		}
	}
	
	function updateCountdownHTML() {
		var 
			daysElem = document.querySelectorAll(".ME .days .number"),
			hoursElem = document.querySelectorAll(".ME .hours .number"),
			minsElem = document.querySelectorAll(".ME .mins .number"),
			secsElem = document.querySelectorAll(".ME .secs .number");

		try{
			formatNumber(daysElem, days);
			formatNumber(hoursElem, hours);
			formatNumber(minsElem, mins);
			formatNumber(secsElem, secs);
		}
		catch(ex) {
			/* In case there are still tasks on the event queue when 
			we replace the script during a resync */
		}
		
	}
	
	var dontCount = (days < 0 || hours < 0 || mins < 0) || (days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins == 0);
	if(dontCount) {
		days = 0; hours = 0; mins = 0;
		updateCountdownHTML();
		return;
	}
		
	intervalId = setInterval(countdown, 1000);
	
	function fetchCountdown() {		
		$.ajax({  
				type: "GET",
				url : "/gsol/SITE/JSP/HOMEPAGE-TS-COUNTDOWN.jsp?show="+show,
				dataType : "html",
				async: true,
				success: function(data){
					/* About to replace the script - clear all existing tasks in event queue */
					clearInterval(intervalId);
					clearInterval(resyncIntervalId);
					$("#countdown-placeholder"+show).html(data);
				}
			});
	}
	
	/* Re-synchronize on window focus */
	$(window).on("focus", function(){
		if(window["ST_focusIntervalId_ME"]) { 
			return; 
		}
		else {
			fetchCountdown();
			window["ST_focusIntervalId_ME"] = 
				setTimeout(function(){ window["ST_focusIntervalId_ME"] = null; }, FOCUS_EVENT_DELAY);
		}
	});
	
	/* Re-synchronize every 10 minutes */
	resyncIntervalId = setInterval(fetchCountdown, RESYNC_INTERVAL);
	
})();
</script>
</div>

<p class="date">October 27-30, 2019</p>
<p class="addr">AsiaWorld-Expo, Hong Kong SAR</p>
<div id="countdown-placeholderGH">
<!-- countdown -->
<style>
	.countdown-cont{width:110%;margin:15px -5% 0;text-align:center;}
	.countdown{padding:5px 5%;border:solid #ce3f51 1px;border-radius:8px;display:inline-block;}
	.countdown > div{display:inline-block;box-sizing:border-box;}
	.countdown .number{padding:2px;margin-left:0;font-size:28px;font-weight:700;display:inline-block;text-align:center;color:#ce3f51;}
	.countdown .label{padding:2px 0 2px 0;font-size:12px;font-weight:400;text-align:center;display:block;color:#666;}
	.countdown .sep{display:inline-block;vertical-align:top;font-size:30px;font-weight:700;color:#666;}
	.countdown .sep::after{content:":";font-weight:normal;}
	@media screen and (max-width:1023px) {
		.countdown{padding:5px 3%;}
		.countdown .number, .countdown .sep{font-size:18px;}
	}
</style>
<div class="countdown-cont">
<div class="countdown GH">
<div class="days">
<span class="number">3</span>
<span class="number">0</span>
<span class="label">DAYS</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="hours">
<span class="number">1</span>
<span class="number">7</span>
<span class="label">HOURS</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="mins">
<span class="number">5</span>
<span class="number">5</span>
<span class="label">MINUTES</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="secs">
<span class="number">2</span>
<span class="number">8</span>
<span class="label">SECONDS</span>
</div>
</div>

<script>
(function(){
	var 
		FOCUS_EVENT_DELAY = 10000,
		RESYNC_INTERVAL = 10*60000;
	
	var 
		show = "GH",
		days = 30,
		hours = 17,
		mins = 55,
		secs = 29,
		intervalId = null,
		resyncIntervalId = null;
		
	function formatNumber(elem, n) {
		elem[0].innerHTML = Math.floor(n / 10);
		elem[1].innerHTML = n % 10;
	}
		
	function countdown() {
		
		if(days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins == 0) {
			clearInterval(intervalId); return;
		}
		
		--secs;
		if(secs < 0) {
			secs = 59;
			--mins;
		}
		if(mins < 0) { mins = 59; --hours; }
		if(hours < 0){ hours = 23;--days; }
		if(days < 0) { days = 0; }
		
		updateCountdownHTML();
		
		if(days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins <= 5) {
			clearInterval(intervalId);
			/* Remove countdown once time reaches 4 mins */
			$("#countdown-placeholder"+show).html("");
			$(".TS_GH .GS_TS_btn").css("bottom", "100px");
			return;
		}
	}
	
	function updateCountdownHTML() {
		var 
			daysElem = document.querySelectorAll(".GH .days .number"),
			hoursElem = document.querySelectorAll(".GH .hours .number"),
			minsElem = document.querySelectorAll(".GH .mins .number"),
			secsElem = document.querySelectorAll(".GH .secs .number");

		try{
			formatNumber(daysElem, days);
			formatNumber(hoursElem, hours);
			formatNumber(minsElem, mins);
			formatNumber(secsElem, secs);
		}
		catch(ex) {
			/* In case there are still tasks on the event queue when 
			we replace the script during a resync */
		}
		
	}
	
	var dontCount = (days < 0 || hours < 0 || mins < 0) || (days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins == 0);
	if(dontCount) {
		days = 0; hours = 0; mins = 0;
		updateCountdownHTML();
		return;
	}
		
	intervalId = setInterval(countdown, 1000);
	
	function fetchCountdown() {		
		$.ajax({  
				type: "GET",
				url : "/gsol/SITE/JSP/HOMEPAGE-TS-COUNTDOWN.jsp?show="+show,
				dataType : "html",
				async: true,
				success: function(data){
					/* About to replace the script - clear all existing tasks in event queue */
					clearInterval(intervalId);
					clearInterval(resyncIntervalId);
					$("#countdown-placeholder"+show).html(data);
				}
			});
	}
	
	/* Re-synchronize on window focus */
	$(window).on("focus", function(){
		if(window["ST_focusIntervalId_GH"]) { 
			return; 
		}
		else {
			fetchCountdown();
			window["ST_focusIntervalId_GH"] = 
				setTimeout(function(){ window["ST_focusIntervalId_GH"] = null; }, FOCUS_EVENT_DELAY);
		}
	});
	
	/* Re-synchronize every 10 minutes */
	resyncIntervalId = setInterval(fetchCountdown, RESYNC_INTERVAL);
	
})();
</script>
</div>

<div class="banner bg_lazy" data-original="//s.globalsources.com/ST/i/GSHP_TSBG_FA.JPG">
<h3 class="conTit">Hong Kong SAR largest fashion sourcing show!</h3>
<ol class="txtlist">
<li><span class="dot"></span><span>Fashion Bags</span></li>
<li><span class="dot"></span><span>Footwear</span></li>

<li><span class="dot"></span><span>Apparel</span></li>
<li><span class="dot"></span><span>Textiles &amp; Trimmings</span></li>
</ol>
<p class="date">October 27-30, 2019</p>
<p class="addr">AsiaWorld-Expo, Hong Kong SAR</p>
<div id="countdown-placeholderFA">
<!-- countdown -->
<style>
	.countdown-cont{width:110%;margin:15px -5% 0;text-align:center;}
	.countdown{padding:5px 5%;border:solid #ce3f51 1px;border-radius:8px;display:inline-block;}
	.countdown > div{display:inline-block;box-sizing:border-box;}
	.countdown .number{padding:2px;margin-left:0;font-size:28px;font-weight:700;display:inline-block;text-align:center;color:#ce3f51;}
	.countdown .label{padding:2px 0 2px 0;font-size:12px;font-weight:400;text-align:center;display:block;color:#666;}
	.countdown .sep{display:inline-block;vertical-align:top;font-size:30px;font-weight:700;color:#666;}
	.countdown .sep::after{content:":";font-weight:normal;}
	@media screen and (max-width:1023px) {
		.countdown{padding:5px 3%;}
		.countdown .number, .countdown .sep{font-size:18px;}
	}
</style>
<div class="countdown-cont">
<div class="countdown FA">
<div class="days">
<span class="number">3</span>
<span class="number">0</span>
<span class="label">DAYS</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="hours">
<span class="number">1</span>
<span class="number">7</span>
<span class="label">HOURS</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="mins">
<span class="number">5</span>
<span class="number">5</span>
<span class="label">MINUTES</span>
</div>
<span class="sep"></span>
<div class="secs">
<span class="number">2</span>
<span class="number">8</span>
<span class="label">SECONDS</span>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<script>
(function(){
	var 
		FOCUS_EVENT_DELAY = 10000,
		RESYNC_INTERVAL = 10*60000;
	
	var 
		show = "FA",
		days = 30,
		hours = 17,
		mins = 55,
		secs = 29,
		intervalId = null,
		resyncIntervalId = null;
		
	function formatNumber(elem, n) {
		elem[0].innerHTML = Math.floor(n / 10);
		elem[1].innerHTML = n % 10;
	}
		
	function countdown() {
		
		if(days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins == 0) {
			clearInterval(intervalId); return;
		}
		
		--secs;
		if(secs < 0) {
			secs = 59;
			--mins;
		}
		if(mins < 0) { mins = 59; --hours; }
		if(hours < 0){ hours = 23;--days; }
		if(days < 0) { days = 0; }
		
		updateCountdownHTML();
		
		if(days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins <= 5) {
			clearInterval(intervalId);
			/* Remove countdown once time reaches 4 mins */
			$("#countdown-placeholder"+show).html("");
			$(".TS_FA .GS_TS_btn").css("bottom", "100px");
			return;
		}
	}
	
	function updateCountdownHTML() {
		var 
			daysElem = document.querySelectorAll(".FA .days .number"),
			hoursElem = document.querySelectorAll(".FA .hours .number"),
			minsElem = document.querySelectorAll(".FA .mins .number"),
			secsElem = document.querySelectorAll(".FA .secs .number");

		try{
			formatNumber(daysElem, days);
			formatNumber(hoursElem, hours);
			formatNumber(minsElem, mins);
			formatNumber(secsElem, secs);
		}
		catch(ex) {
			/* In case there are still tasks on the event queue when 
			we replace the script during a resync */
		}
		
	}
	
	var dontCount = (days < 0 || hours < 0 || mins < 0) || (days == 0 && hours == 0 && mins == 0);
	if(dontCount) {
		days = 0; hours = 0; mins = 0;
		updateCountdownHTML();
		return;
	}
		
	intervalId = setInterval(countdown, 1000);
	
	function fetchCountdown() {		
		$.ajax({  
				type: "GET",
				url : "/gsol/SITE/JSP/HOMEPAGE-TS-COUNTDOWN.jsp?show="+show,
				dataType : "html",
				async: true,
				success: function(data){
					/* About to replace the script - clear all existing tasks in event queue */
					clearInterval(intervalId);
					clearInterval(resyncIntervalId);
					$("#countdown-placeholder"+show).html(data);
				}
			});
	}
	
	/* Re-synchronize on window focus */
	$(window).on("focus", function(){
		if(window["ST_focusIntervalId_FA"]) { 
			return; 
		}
		else {
			fetchCountdown();
			window["ST_focusIntervalId_FA"] = 
				setTimeout(function(){ window["ST_focusIntervalId_FA"] = null; }, FOCUS_EVENT_DELAY);
		}
	});
	
	/* Re-synchronize every 10 minutes */
	resyncIntervalId = setInterval(fetchCountdown, RESYNC_INTERVAL);
	
})();
</script>
</div>
